Battalion Commander Hu led his team to encircle and suppress them, killing many hostages and capturing many bandit ships. Yesterday, it returned victoriously to Jiang and was stationed at the Jiedai Temple outside the East Gate.

The Convicted Robber in a Local Robbery Case Appeals: Gu Changbu Cloth Store in Shengjia Warehouse in the city (the store whose young son was kidnapped on the 10th of this month) was robbed of 55 yuan in banknotes, 26 yuan in silver, and 76 cents in small silver on the night of August 16th of the previous year. Wang Naiqing was arrested by the county police, and sentenced to nine years in prison. Now the bandit is not satisfied and has appealed. With the approval of the Wuxian Local Court, a hearing is scheduled for the 21st of this month.

Suzhou 83

Commander-in-Chief Chiang Commends Hu Zuyu by Telegram: Zhang Zhaohua, the leader of the Haizhou bandit gang in Yangcheng Lake, was shot and captured by the Water Public Security Guerrilla Team in Weiting Mountain and sent to the Guangmin Hospital in Suzhou for treatment. The Chief of Staff of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters, Director Deng of the Military Law Department, went to the Guangmin Hospital to interrogate the criminal, proving that Zhang Zhaohua was indeed a bandit leader. It is learned that the Chief of Staff specially ordered soldiers to go to the Guangmin Hospital at about 2:00 PM today (17th) to escort Zhang Zhaohua to the headquarters for punishment. As for Hu, the Chief of Staff, who completely annihilated Zhang's bandit gang in Yangcheng Lake in recent days, reported to the Nanjing Commander-in-Chief. Now, Commander-in-Chief Chiang has sent a telegram today (17th) to commend him.

Bandit Suppression Troops Recapture Si'an: More than 1,000 bandits, led by bandit leader Zhang Minggao, were discovered in the border area between Anhui and Zhejiang. On the 15th, they captured Si'an. Hangzhou Yi, the commander of the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Security Team, and Zhong Huan, the commander of the West District of the Taihu Bandit Suppression, led their troops to bravely suppress them. On the 16th at noon, they recaptured Si'an. Several important bandit leaders were killed in this battle. Commander Zhong telegraphed the Bandit Suppression Headquarters on the evening of the 16th. The original telegram is recorded as follows: (1) Bandit leader Zhang Minggao led 1,000 bandits and attacked and captured Si'an. (2) The Hangzhou regiment suffered the loss of two platoons due to the disparity in numbers. (3) On the 16th, the Hangzhou regimental commander led three companies to join forces with Battalion Commander Feng of the same regiment, leading the 3rd, 4th, 6th, and 7th companies, and fought fiercely with the bandits near Kongshan. (4) The bandits resisted stubbornly for five hours. Our army won a great victory and recaptured Si'an at noon. (5) In this battle, the bandit regimental commander Wang, the bandit adjutant Lin Guangyin, a well-known knife bandit, Yu, the confidant of bandit camp commander Zhang and a former instructor of the defense regiment, and more than 300 other bandits were killed on the spot. (6) Countless rifles and broadswords were seized, and more than 100 people were captured. (7) The remaining bandits were scattered in small groups, mostly fleeing south. (8) Only one or two soldiers in my Zhong regiment were injured.

Hu Zuyu Departs to Suppress Bandits in the West District: Hu Zuyu, the commander of the 13th Brigade of the Fifth Division and the Chief of Staff of Taihu Bandit Suppression, because the large-scale lake bandits in the Wu Kunjiang counties of the East District have been wiped out, and the bandit forces in the West District and the border area between Jiangsu and Zhejiang are still strong, specially led his troops from Suzhou on the morning of the 17th at 9:00 AM, taking the Baosu and Zhaowu shallow-water warships to patrol the West District.

Temporary Detention Center for Prisoners Established: The temporary detention center for prisoners in Jiangsu Province was established on the 15th. Today (17th), the Higher Court will abolish the preparatory office organized by Wei Bangzhen and Shi Zechen and report it to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for record.

Changshu 84

Robbery by Bandits in Lu Yuan Town: At 10:00 PM on the 14th of this month, fifty or sixty pirates landed at the Jinggangkou outside Lu Yuan from the sea. At that time, there was an offshore naval patrol boat outside the port. The pirates first went to the patrol boat, forcibly seizing four rifles, a small cannon, and injuring one police officer. After the pirates succeeded, they proceeded to Lu Yuan Town and first went to the home of Town Mayor Yi Ren, who had previously organized the defense regiment, and all the military equipment was in Yi's possession. That night, Yi was away on business, and the pirates went to Yi's residence, calling for the surrender of weapons. They injured Yi's mother and tied up Yi's daughter. Yi's mother handed over four rifles to the pirates, who took them away. They then broke in and forced the surrender of a Mauser pistol and proceeded to the north street of Lu Yuan, first robbing Sun Jinheng's cloth store. The store owner, Sun Yongming, was shot and killed by the pirates. They kidnapped an old man, a son, and a daughter, as well as a temple caretaker, a total of four people, and lost 300 yuan. Next, they robbed the Yifengtai South Goods Store, kidnapping one son and three employees, and the Xinchangyu Jinghuo Store, kidnapping one employee and one apprentice, losing 86 yuan, and a package of crepe yarn (worth about 400 yuan). At the Dingchangyi Jinghuo Store, they kidnapped the store owner Zhang Mingfu and one apprentice, losing 12 bolts of silk and satin and more than 40 yuan. They destroyed the belongings of the Xie Da Rice Store and took away a horn, but did not kidnap anyone. They kidnapped the store employee Chen Yichang from the Xiehe Fish Shop, losing 1,534 yuan and 86 cents in small silver. At the Qian Changding's house (the homeowner and others were sightseeing in Hangzhou), the losses are unknown. At the Wangjianglou Teahouse, they injured employee Guo Fubao, who was sent to Changshu Hospital for treatment. The losses are unknown. The Lu Yuan Town Office destroyed a telephone and cut off communication between the city and the countryside. Before leaving, the pirates went to various opium dens to search for opium pipes, about a bundle. After midnight, they still left from Dajinggangkou. Yesterday, the county government, according to the report of District Chief Xu, ordered the Public Security Bureau Investigation Team to rush to the town to investigate in detail.

Wuxi 85

Meningitis Spreads in Urban and Rural Areas: In the past week, there have been continuous rainy days, and the weather is abnormal. Meningitis, which kills like a tiger, has been seen spreading in the city. Many residents suffer from this disease, especially children.

Robbery by Bandits in Songfengli: Xu Jinhe, a farmer in Songfengli, Tianshang City, in the county, is engaged in farming and has a small fortune. On the night before last, at about 1:00 AM, five or six bandits suddenly came, wearing short clothes, speaking in local accents, and holding knives, sticks, flashlights, and other instruments. They kicked open the door of Xu's house, broke in, ransacked the boxes and chests, and searched wantonly. After half an hour, they took the stolen goods and left. After the incident, it was found that 15 yuan in cash, 21,000 copper coins, and gold and silver jewelry and clothing worth about 450 yuan were robbed.

Suspect in Jailbreak Case Brought to Wuxi: The County Detention Sub-Office experienced a jailbreak by prisoners on the night of the 26th of last month. After the Higher Court sent a committee to Wuxi to investigate, it was found that Liu Yinqiu, the clerk of the Wuxi Detention Sub-Office, and Meng Yugen, the former warden of the sub-office and the current warden of the Yangzhong County Detention Center, were both suspects. After ordering them to be guarded, Sun County Magistrate sent Wu Rongsheng, the chief of the Political Police Team, to Yangzhong County to bring Meng Yugen back to Wuxi yesterday. Chief Judge Zhou conducted a hearing. Meng confessed that the four waistbands issued to the prisoners being transported had never existed. As for Zhang Aqi, the escaped prisoner, who usually cooked and carried water in the detention center, he had a waistband, etc. After the interrogation, he was taken into custody and it was decided that Meng Yugen and Liu Yinqiu would be sent to the Wuxian District Court for interrogation within the next few days.

Changzhou 86

Assassination Case Occurs at Mahang Bridge: Jiang Genyao, of Mahang Bridge in Wuyi County, used to make a living by operating a shuttle boat. Recently, due to the dredging of the Cailing Port, the shuttle boat stopped running. Jiang went to the city to pick up goods, but on April 7th, after going to the city, he did not return. His family searched without success. On the morning of the 15th, a male corpse was found in a ditch in Puhang Village nearby. Jiang's wife, Yang, rushed to see it and confirmed that it was her husband, Genyao, floating on the surface of the water. The body was pulled up, and there were rope marks on the neck and cotton wool stuffed in the mouth, indicating that he had been murdered and his body dumped in the ditch. The town mayor of the town, Xu Ziyou, was reported and reported to the County Court on the 16th to send personnel to investigate and arrest the murderer.

Theft in the Vicinity of Nan Zhai Town: In the vicinity of Nan Zhai Town in the eighth district of Wuyi County, there have been many robbery cases in the past month. After the district office secretly dispatched various guard teams to investigate, Yang Zhaosheng, a robber, was arrested on the evening of the 14th. He confessed to the robbery of Guanzhuang and confessed that the leaders were Zhou Jianrong, Jiang Xiangying, and more than ten others. On the morning of the 15th, during a storm, the members of each team arrested Zhou Jianrong and Jiang Xiangying at the address and escorted them to the county for interrogation. After County Magistrate Wu interrogated them, he ordered them to be chained and imprisoned.

Jiangyin 87

Dispute over Welcoming Guests Leads to Rice Dispute: The day before yesterday (15th), a rice boat arrived from Beiwai, carrying more than 200 dan of rough and white rice. The rice merchant Pan Jinrui transported it from Anhui to the port and first contacted Yin Ruiyuan firm, who purchased more than 100 dan at a price of 14.5 yuan. Then Wu Hengsheng contacted him and offered a price of 14.55 yuan. Yesterday morning, Yin Ruiyuan could add 5 cents and unloaded another 37 dan. The rice was then transferred to Huangtian Port to the east, entered Huangshan Port, and unloaded at Yifengheng outside the East Gate. At about 8:00 AM, Wu Hengsheng found 55 dan of rough rice and 33 dan of white rice that could be transferred to a large boat in the middle of the river by sampan, intending to sell it to Xiagang. The owner of Yin Ruiyuan firm pointed out that the rice on the boat was suspected of being exported and reported it to the Public Security Bureau, which ordered the police to detain it. A meeting of rice merchants was convened at the Rice Industry Association. As a result, Wu Hengsheng transported rice for export, and there was no definite evidence. Yin Ruiyuan also had rice transported east from the Yangtze River, but Wu Hengsheng should not have violated the industry rules by taking over customers. It was agreed that Wu Hengsheng would donate 251 yuan, which would be allocated by the association to the price stabilization bureau in this district to specialize in helping the poor. The detained rice can only be sold in this industry. The matter was finally settled.

Killing Grandfather to Force Marriage of Wife and Niece: Zhang Shaoqing, the bandit leader from Taixing, also known as Weng Tianliang, was arrested in Cheng. Yesterday, it was learned that the bandit had a wife, Chen, also known as Duo Guniang, who also lived in Jiangyin. She was the niece of the victim Xu Huang. Her father's name was Chen Shaoqing, and her mother had died early. She was forced to marry in October of last year. The night before last, she saw her uncle crying in the Datong Hotel, saying that she had been separated from her family and could not find death. She currently has more than 400 yuan deposited in the Fuchangren Dyeing Workshop, but it is difficult to withdraw it for a while. Xu Huang helped her sort it out and took 200 yuan in silver, and the rest will be returned in two installments during the Dragon Boat Festival and the Mid-Autumn Festival. On the afternoon of the 16th, Chen and her uncle Xu Huang returned to Taixing together. It is said that Chen is still six months pregnant.

Zhenjiang 88

New Director of Finance Bureau Takes Office: Ren Yunkui, the director of the Zhenjiang County Finance Bureau, was transferred to the office and replaced by Wang Zhao Jia. It is learned that Wang arrived at the bureau yesterday to take office.

Tenants Oppose Rent Increase at Wanjie Hall: The property of Wanjie Hall in Zhenjiang has considerable annual income. Since the provincial government moved to Zhenjiang last year, the price of housing has risen. The tenants have already reluctantly increased their rent by 30%. Recently, when demolishing houses to make way for land, the rent collector of the hall seized the opportunity to speak to the long-term tenants, intending to increase the current rent by more than 50%. Because the tenants could not bear the harassment, some people advocated going to the Civil Affairs Office to inquire about the ban issued by the Civil Affairs Office on April 10 of last year and this year, and went to the Party Department to complain. If the rent collector threatens to terminate the contract or relies on his power to force a transfer, the tenants will implement a joint tenants' association as a fundamental defense measure.

Yangzhou 89

Robbery Case Involving Killing Grandfather and Abducting Grandson: At 2:00 AM this morning (16th), at the Xue Shunxing firewood shed at Mabaidu Ferry outside the South Gate, more than ten armed bandits suddenly broke in, ransacking boxes and chests. Xue Guangfu saw the bandits abducting his six-year-old grandson (named Jin Lingzi) from his daughter-in-law's room, so he risked his life to rush forward to snatch him, but was shot twice and fell to the ground and died. After obtaining the hostage, the bandits took the other stolen goods and went south. According to the gang of bandits, they were heavily armed. In addition to countless rifles, there were also five Mauser pistols. Most of them spoke with a Qingzhun accent.

Arrested for Smoking, Mistaken for Bandits: The Yangzhou County Public Security Bureau has been reorganized extensively. Only one of the five branch offices in the city has been retained, and the branch chiefs who have been laid off or transferred are all panicked. Yesterday (15th) was the date of implementation of the reorganization. Two days before the handover, Guo Hanzhang, the chief of the Second Branch in the city, extensively searched for smoking and gambling dens within his jurisdiction. On the night of the 14th, because he arrested a smoking monk, he even used a gold bracelet to represent the fine. Last night (15th), he arrested a smoking den at the home of Dr. Geng Xiaoting in Gengjia Lane. A business group was stationed at the entrance of the lane. Hearing the police, they suspected that there were bandits, so they surrounded Geng's house and exchanged fire for half an hour. The neighbors were terrified. It is now heard that the leading police chief and the reporter of the bureau have been sent to the County Government by Director Zhao of the General Bureau for legal disposal.

Division of Authority Between Police and Public Security: Chen, the County Magistrate of this county, issued an order stating that the investigation and arrest of smoking and gambling should be the responsibility of the public security personnel, and the police team should be responsible for suppressing bandits and arresting criminals. Recently, it has been learned that the police team is extorting money by investigating smoking and gambling, which is very inappropriate. Yesterday (15th), the previous order was reiterated, prohibiting the police team from interfering in smoking and gambling incidents, in order to emphasize the legal order.

New News on Unified Finance: The Jiangdu County Government, according to the resolution on unified local finance at the Second Administrative Conference, instructed the Finance Bureau to comply. Currently, the Finance Bureau reports that, in addition to the transfer of the collection of various donations and taxes from the Public Security Bureau, the various donations and taxes collected by the Education Bureau are still handled by the Education Fund Management Office, and no reply has been received. Yesterday (15th), a request was specially submitted to the County Government, which promptly instructed the Education Bureau to comply with the previous order. At the same time, the directors of the Construction and Finance Bureaus were ordered to jointly discuss and reply whether the slaughter and construction special donations collected by the Construction Bureau are related to the unified finance plan in order to review and handle the matter.

Nantong 90

County Police Force Implements Reorganization: Jin Juechen, appointed by the Civil Affairs Department as the head of the Nantong County Police Brigade, will dismiss all armed unit soldiers, eliminate undesirable elements, and reorganize them into two companies. Li Hanbin will be appointed as the deputy commander. The county will review and inspect the changes, enforce strict training, prohibit police officers from leaving the camp, and procure foreign rice to relieve the famine. A rice shortage has occurred in the town, with market prices soaring to twenty-five yuan per stone. The financial community is currently raising funds to purchase 18,000 bags of foreign rice in Shanghai for distribution as relief on the 16th.

Punishment for Bandits Captured in Eastern Villages: The military police, while suppressing bandits in the eastern villages, have successively captured over 180 male and female bandits, who were then handed over to the Local Pacification Bureau for interrogation. Over thirty individuals with particularly serious involvement have been reported by the county government to the provincial authorities for review and punishment, while those with insufficient evidence of criminal activity have been granted bail.

Deadline for National Salvation Fund Remittance: The former National Salvation Association of Nantong is still collecting the National Salvation Fund. The current County Reorganization Committee, acting on provincial orders to investigate regular meetings, has resolved to set a deadline of ten days for those handling the funds to provide a clear accounting. Failure to comply within the deadline will result in a report to the province for a wanted order.

Hangzhou 91

Bandits with Broadswords Flee into Anhui Province: A portion of Anhui bandits, after fleeing into Zhejiang, joined forces with the Broadsword Society bandits of Changxing, totaling about 2,000 people. They looted Sian Town the day before yesterday and occupied it. The stationed military police were too weak to resist, resulting in significant losses. Subsequently, the Second Regiment of the Security Brigade dispatched troops to fiercely suppress them, engaging in fierce battles all day. On the night of the 15th, Sian was recaptured, and the bandits fled into Anhui Province. The Hangzhou Regiment Commander sent a lengthy telegram to the province yesterday.

Allocation for Construction Bonds Issuance: Zhejiang Province is issuing construction bonds totaling ten million yuan. The Finance Department has already assigned the quota. It is said that Hangzhou and Ningbo each have been allocated one million yuan, Jiaxing and other counties have been assigned 350,000 yuan, and the remaining amounts are still being allocated.

Shangyu 92

Fierce Battle between Soldiers and Bandits in Shan'ao: On the evening of the 14th, at about 10 p.m., seventeen or eighteen bandits suddenly arrived at the home of He Caizhao in Shan'ao, Eastern Township. All were armed with wooden-holstered guns, broke down the main door, and rushed upstairs, engaging in unrestrained looting. Caizhao's cousin, Caifeng, lived across from his younger brother, Wangheng. Hearing the commotion inside his brother's house and the bandits firing their guns outside the door as a show of force, he realized something was amiss and escaped through the back door, running to Yonghe Market, about a mile from the village. He reported to the County Defense Team and Anti-Smuggling Team stationed there, requesting their assistance. By the time the soldiers arrived at Shan'ao, the bandits had moved from He Caizhao's house into Caifeng's residence. The soldiers then opened fire, and the bandits returned fire, resulting in a fierce battle lasting over ten minutes. The bandits, unable to withstand the pressure, fled towards Qingxian Ridge and Fengding Gang. In this incident, He Caizhao's house was looted of clothing and gold rings and hairpins deposited by his cousin Haichao, totaling over 300 yuan in losses. Because the soldiers arrived at He Caifeng's house before it could be looted, it was spared from damage. The victim has already filed a loss report on the 15th, requesting the county government to conduct an on-site investigation and dispatch additional troops to be stationed there to maintain order.

Ningbo 93

Municipal Government Discusses Lowering Rice Prices: Following the request from the Yin County Party Headquarters to lower rice prices and alleviate the livelihood of the common people, the Ningbo Municipal Government convened a meeting yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. in the government's library, gathering representatives from rice businesses and chambers of commerce to discuss solutions. The results were: (1) Within three days, each rice storehouse must voluntarily lower the minimum rice price as much as possible. If the rice price cannot be lowered within three days, the municipal and county governments will reconvene the meeting to discuss solutions. (2) Fixed rice shipments between Shanghai and Ningbo must be delivered in Ningbo and cannot be unloaded in Shanghai.

Opposition to Japanese Naval Exercises: The Japanese fleet intends to conduct spring naval exercises in the waters near Zhoushan in our country's territorial sea, showing utter disregard for our national sovereignty. All civil groups in Ningbo expressed extreme indignation upon hearing this news. Yesterday, the County Party Headquarters resolved to submit a request to the central government for expulsion. The Journalists Association has also sent a telegram of opposition.

News of the Railway Minister's Visit to Ningbo: According to transportation news, Railway Minister Sun Ke and Director Liu Weihuan are scheduled to arrive in Ningbo from Shanghai on the 17th to inspect the Yin-Feng Motor Road and the Yong-Cao Railway, then travel to Hangzhou to visit West Lake.

Xiaoshan 94

Monk from the Zhiyuan Temple Disappears: The Zhiyuan Temple in Xiaocheng is a renowned ancient temple in our Xiao area. The temple's real estate and monthly income amount to no less than tens of thousands of yuan. Recently, due to heavy taxation and difficult expenses, the temple's abbot, Changming, suddenly disappeared a few days ago. Some say that the monk was involved in a certain case and absconded with funds. The truth remains unknown.

Father and Son Die from Eating Dead Sheep: A resident of Shadi Qijia Sha, surnamed Wen, in Xiaoshan, had a dead sheep. On the 13th, he and his son cooked and ate it. Soon after, they suffered from stomach pain and diarrhea. Despite his wife's best efforts to treat them, there was no improvement. The father and son died simultaneously the next day.

Robbery in Nanwu: The home of Zhu Yousan, a resident of Nanwu, located on the border of Shaoxing and Xiaoshan, was suddenly raided by more than ten bandits on the night of the 12th. They broke into the house and engaged in unrestrained looting. In addition to the loss of over 300 yuan in clothing and ornaments, they also stole two stones of white rice and five dou of broad beans. The head farmhand was also slashed in the head, resulting in profuse bleeding.

Construction Bonds Fundraising Begins: The Xiaoshan County Government has received the provincial regulations for raising construction bonds and, recognizing the urgent need for construction, is proceeding with fundraising. Xiaoshan's assigned fundraising amount is 200,000 yuan, to be raised in stages and meet the quota on time. County Magistrate Du plans to organize a fundraising committee and allocate fundraising quotas to each township.

Shaoxing 95

Guild Merchants Telegram Requesting Exemption from Construction Bond Allocation: All the salt merchants in Eastern Zhejiang, due to insufficient ability to raise construction bonds, telegraphed the Zhejiang Salt Transport Commissioner on the 15th, stating that upon receiving the Commissioner's letter ordering the Zhejiang salt merchants to subscribe to 800,000 yuan of Zhejiang Province construction bonds, they were extremely alarmed. In recent years, salt sales have been sluggish, and public bonds have been paid in installments, resulting in heavy debts and no access to loans. The Commissioner is fully aware of the merchants' various hardships. Therefore, they earnestly request the Commissioner to show compassion for the merchants' difficulties and relay to the Chairman a request for exemption. They also ask a wealthy merchant in Shanghai to explain the situation of Shaoxing merchants' impoverishment and lack of access to loans to Chairman Zhang and request him to consider the merchants' difficulties and allow for a change, exempting them from the allocation.

Third Day of the National Education Conference 96

Chairman Chiang's Speech Emphasizes Agricultural Education

Discussion on Preliminary Plans for Implementing Compulsory Education

Second General Assembly Held Yesterday Afternoon

Group Review Meetings Held in the Morning

Yesterday's National Education Conference 97

▲ Conference Situation

The second general assembly was held yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. The venue arrangement was similar to yesterday, except that a dozen flower pots were placed around the perimeter, filled with various flowers, pleasing to the eye. On the members' seats were copies of Mr. Liu Dabai's "White House Literary Model," presented by the World Book Company, and "Measures for Uniform Official Document Formats for Educational Institutions," recently published by the Ministry of Education and presented by the Zhonghua Book Company, for members' study. The seating arrangements for the members had been drawn yesterday, so when the time for the meeting approached, the members arrived in succession and prepared for the meeting.

▲ Members Present

Ma Hetian, Huang Shiheng, Song Deqian, Liu Shilin, Zhang Hongjian, Xu Shoushang, Song Binggong, Zeng Guangming, Xie Shuying, Lu Dianyang, Sun Zuosu, Sun Shouzhi, Sun Huiqing, Tang Maoge, Jiang Ji, Jiang Menglin, Chen Bulei, Yang Zhongming, Feng Bingkui, Yang Xingfo, Ku Qijun, Zhang Mojun, Sun Shiren, Gu Shusen, Chen Heqin, Zheng Hongnian, Zhong Rongguang, Wei Tingsheng, Hu Shuhua, Zhang Xinhai, Wu Jiaxiang, Wang Bingheng, Zhu Jingnong, Jiang Shaomo, Xiong Mengfei, Zhao Naichuan, Weng De, Li Zheng, Zhao Chunqing, Huang Dujie, Qian He, Liu Cixiao, Qiu Zhenzhong, Zhang Honglie, Meng Xiancheng, Wang Maozu, Chen Dezheng, Yu Ziyi, Wang Shengzu, Shao Peizi, Li Quanshi, Xu Jijie, Jin Zengcheng, Lei Peihong, Wei Que, Liao Shicheng, Wu Heling, Song Baoqin, Chen Rongjing, Liu Fazeng, Ou Yuanhuai, Sun Guiding, Mei Zhengyuan, Tan Xihong, Nie Tiren, Yu Qingtang, Chen Jianxiao, Zhuang Zexuan, Gong Zizhi, Wang Xiaofan, Peng Qingpeng, Tao Xuan, Dai Xiujun, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Zhensheng, Wang Ruyi, Chen Hexian, Li Yuying, Liu Zhanen, Dai Chao, Chen Zhengmo, Huang Jianzhong, Yang Fang, Jin Baoshan, Xie Yingzhou, He Siyuan, Lu Yougang, Wang Shinai, Li Zhaohuan, Xiang Xiongxiao.

Guests present: Jiang Zhongzheng, Qian Yonghe, Xie Dazhi, Zhang Zhenyu, Liu Fenzi, Miao Qiusheng, Zhang Linggao, Zhao Yuren, Chen Yuqing, Wu Shuyi, Li Bojia, and dozens of reporters from various newspapers.

▲ Chairman Chiang's Speech

At the start of the meeting, Chairman Chiang entered the venue in casual clothes and ascended the podium. Minister Jiang announced the opening of the meeting and invited Chairman Jiang of the National Government to deliver a speech, as follows:

"I am very honored to participate in the second National Education Conference today. I do not have much research on education and dare not contribute much to everyone. However, I personally have many feelings about domestic education recently, so I will share them with you.

(1) The work of the National Revolution has not yet been completed, and its greatest foundation is actually education. If this foundation is not solid, the danger is very great. Therefore, Chinese education should be reformed and perfected as soon as possible, so that the general youth can stand under the Three Principles of the People and work together. There are many bad trends in the country today, and it is up to us to reform them through revolutionary means. Since the May Fourth Movement, revolutionary comrades have paid more attention to destruction and not enough to construction. This is due to time constraints and not choosing means. There are indeed unavoidable difficulties. Although the era of destruction has passed, the academic atmosphere in the country is still bad. This is the result of today's education, and the bad results cannot be said to be the fruit planted in the past. Because the National Revolution must succeed, it is important to study how to implement and build education in the revolutionary process. What time is it now? The time for destruction has passed. If we re-implement education of a destructive nature, it will definitely fail. Education of a constructive nature must take order as a prerequisite. When the Premier went north in the 24th year of the Republic of China, he gave a speech to the Huangpu students, speaking for two hours. The main idea was that party members have no freedom, students have no freedom, so the Premier absolutely does not advocate that students have freedom. I believe that all the bad situations in China today must be blamed on the excessive freedom of students. The effectiveness of education cannot be seen in a day. It can only be seen after ten or twenty years. There is an ancient Chinese saying, 'It takes ten years to grow trees, but a hundred years to cultivate people,' which is a famous saying. Today's education should bear the responsibility for the survival of the nation. Therefore, the principals of various universities and the directors of education departments in various provinces bear a heavy burden, directly and indirectly related to the survival and urgency of the country. We must bear this responsibility to engage in education. The first step is to rectify the academic atmosphere, so that the previous romantic and chaotic phenomena can be swept away, so that the country's century-long plan can be determined. If education can earnestly rectify the academic atmosphere, no matter what resistance there is, the Party Headquarters and the government will support it at all costs, even sacrificing lives. Otherwise, the Chinese academic atmosphere will never be rectified. I hope that the education authorities in various provinces will pay more attention to this kind of revolutionary spirit, to revive the Chinese national spirit and rectify the Chinese academic atmosphere today.

(2) China is an economically backward country and must not imitate foreign countries. It should create an independent education to suit the current national conditions. China is an agricultural country, so agricultural education is the fundamental plan for saving the country and is more important than any other education. We should not regard establishing the country with agriculture as an old saying. In my opinion, agricultural education must be promoted in any case. If it can be realized, there will be results in five or ten years. Only agricultural education can save our Chinese country and realize the Principle of People's Livelihood. Its effectiveness should be above industrial education and commercial education.

(3) The thoughts of young people must also be unified. Therefore, we should pay close attention to party ideology education. It would be a good way for principals of schools at all levels to take charge of party ideology courses to guide the thoughts of young people. Because the principal is a figure of faith in a school, we must rely on the Three Principles of the People to unify political stability and ideological stability. The education inspectors of the education departments of various provinces must pay attention to how the Party ideology education is implemented in various schools. Not only is this what I personally hope for, but also what the comrades of our party deeply hope for."

▲ Conference Implements Preliminary Plans for Compulsory Education

After a ten-minute break, the bell rang to start the meeting. Speaker Jiang read Article 10 of the revised original text of this plan and asked members to discuss it. (1) Zhu Jingnong first said that the revised text has a wider scope than the original text, so it is more perfect. (2) Zhuang Zexuan said that this series is a formal method, and all words like "discretionary change" should be cancelled. (3) Zhu Jingnong continued that the word "change" is used to make activities such as holidays for rural schools and making up for missed lessons for children (4) Zhang Honglie once said that shortening and changing are not the same thing and must be noted. (5) Peng Qingpeng proposed that the amendment should be revised again and the "discretionary shortening" should be deleted, which was seconded by Xu Jifu and the motion was passed. (6) Liao Shicheng said that the two words "change" can still be used because it is convenient for children to study in actual situations. (7) Zhao Naifu said that the original amendment has no major problems, and the word "shorten" can be changed to "extend". (8) Li Quanshi said that the word "shorten" should be cancelled, and "discretionary change" should be used during the school period. During the vote, those who agreed with the amendment by the review committee and the proposal by the members, "But for children who cannot continue to study for four years, they can make discretionary changes," were passed by a majority.

The Focus of the Conference Discussion is on Teacher Training 98

The focus of the conference discussion is on the independence and merger of normal schools. The first National Education Conference decided that the principle of normal schools and middle schools is to be qualified. In this reform plan for national education, it was decided that normal schools that have been merged with middle schools should be gradually separated within the possible scope, considering local conditions. This provision has tended towards the advocacy of independent normal schools. Members are now divided into two factions: one advocates independent normal schools, and the other advocates the joint school of middle schools and normal schools. There will definitely be a big dispute during future discussions. Judging from the current attending members, the majority advocates independence. It is expected that this case will be a point of contention at the general assembly in the coming days. Experts, education directors from various provinces, and all parties in the education sector attach great importance to the issue of joint schools for middle schools and normal schools. It is expected that a debate on the conference floor will be one of the most exciting scenes of this conference.

Committee Review Meetings 99

▲ Second Review Meeting of the Elementary Education Group

▲ Original Plan Slightly Modified

The Second Review Meeting of the Elementary Education Group was attended by committee members Chen Heqin, Yu Ziyi, Wu Yan Yin, Nie Tiren, Xu Shou, and Zhang Honglie, with Zhao Yuren from the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education attending as an observer. The outcome was general approval of the original plan, with slight modifications to several items. The two main points are: (1) The original plan only listed kindergartens under the item of early childhood education. Now it is changed to early childhood education, which should be divided into two types: 1. Kindergartens, 2. Infant care centers. (2) The original plan was missing an item on special education. The review result is that special education should be included, divided into classes for gifted children, classes for children with learning disabilities, and schools for the disabled.

▲ Second Review Meeting of the Overseas Chinese Education Group

▲ Three Important Points

The Second Review Meeting of the Overseas Chinese Education Group was attended by seven members: Zhong Rongguang, Zheng Hongnian, Zhuang Zexuan, Zhao Naichuan, Qian He, Liu Shimu, and Zhu Baoqin. Zheng Hongnian chaired the meeting, and Zhu Baoqin was the recorder. (1) When poor overseas Chinese students return to China and enter national or provincial schools, they may be granted tuition waivers at the discretion of the school upon presentation of proof from an overseas Chinese organization. (2) Funding standards need not follow domestic school regulations to accommodate special circumstances. (3) The summary should be reported to the General Assembly. There are three important points: 1. Request the Ministry of Education to immediately send personnel to inspect the status of overseas Chinese education in various regions, and pay special attention to the selection of inspectors. 2. When inspectors from the Ministry of Education arrive in various regions for inspection, they should work with local overseas Chinese to quickly establish overseas Chinese education associations, paying special attention to the location of the associations. 3. The Overseas Chinese Education Design Committee should be established as soon as possible to solicit opinions from overseas Chinese education associations in various regions and allocate subsidies.

▲ First Review Meeting of the Social Education Group

Starting at 9:00 AM yesterday, the Social Education Group held its first review meeting in Room 102 of the Central Hotel. The review committee members present were Cai Yuanpei, Lei Peihong, Song Binggong, Duanmu Kai, Chen Zhengmo, Peng Baichuan, Chen Chuangxiu, Liu Zhanen, Yu Qingtang, Jiang Ji, Tang Maoru, Ma Bingkui, and Chen Hexian, totaling thirteen people. Lei Peihong was elected as chairman, and Song Binggong served as secretary. The main points of the review results are as follows: 1. Take public education centers and farmer education centers as the center of implementation and experimentation. All libraries, gymnasiums, exhibition halls, lecture halls, etc., should be integrated with public education centers and farmer education centers within the possible range. 2. To train talent, social education departments should be established in normal universities and education colleges of various universities, and provincial education departments should establish social education colleges or public education institutes, as appropriate. 3. Ordinary advanced public schools should be divided into two types: public schools with advanced classes and youth supplementary schools. 4. Industrial and commercial supplementary schools should promote joint management by factories, shops, or other industrial and commercial education institutions in accordance with the Outline of the Workers' Education Plan. Agricultural supplementary schools should be jointly managed by agricultural extension committees, agricultural instructors, or farmer education institutions in accordance with agricultural extension regulations. 5. Literacy training, civic training, and vocational training can be carried out simultaneously in areas with sufficient financial resources, depending on actual circumstances.

▲ Joint Meeting of the Compulsory Education and Teacher Training Groups

The six-year rural normal schools equivalent to secondary school level in the original plan will remain as they are. 2. The rural normal school specialties at or above the high school level in the original plan will be changed to rural normal school teachers. Departments or programs can be set up in university education colleges or normal universities, or specialized rural normal colleges can be established for training, with at least one in each county.

▲ Review Report of the Compulsory Education Group

The group chairman, Zhang Honglie, reported on the proceedings of the previous day and the results of the review, with a total of three revisions. The revised text is listed below:

(1) Objectives: The objective of this plan is to enable school-age children nationwide to receive four years of elementary school education. However, children who cannot continue for four years may be given appropriate accommodations (Note 1), or the duration of their schooling may be shortened (Note 2), and supplementary schools (Note 3) or a "self-study system" (Note 4) may be used to supplement their compulsory education.

(2) Time Limit: It is planned to complete the establishment of teacher training institutions nationwide within five years, and to open 1,500 compulsory education experimental areas in cities and villages during the same period (Note 5), so that all important counties nationwide can start small-scale experiments on compulsory education, which will be gradually promoted year by year until the end of the twentieth year. However, education administrative officers of various provinces and cities may shorten the time limit and complete the work ahead of schedule, depending on local conditions.

Vice-Speaker Chen Hexian, Photo by Guanghua

Lu Dianyang proposed that if the 20-year period is changed to 10 years, problems will arise with teacher training and funding, and it will not be in accordance with the budget plan, so it is appropriate to maintain the original plan and add "(Education administrative officers of various provinces and cities) may implement compulsory education ahead of schedule depending on local conditions." Hu Shuhua seconded the motion, and the motion was passed. Yu Ziyi said that if compulsory education is changed to 10 years, the financial budget will have to bear additional burdens every year, which will cause problems for the national economy. Therefore, it is appropriate to maintain the original plan and add Lu Dianyang's amendment, and special attention should be paid to local wealth. Wei Tingsheng said that the national economic strength has improved more than before, so funding problems may not be difficult. In my opinion, the teacher problem may be more difficult. It is not easy to cultivate teachers in remote areas, so solving the teacher problem cannot be completed in five or six years. Therefore, I still agree with Mr. Lu Dianyang's proposal to consider local conditions and not to raise the issue of teacher training and wealth. Lu Dianyang continued to say that the motivation for the proposal was due to the difficulty in the revision of the review group regarding speeding up things. Therefore, Wang Zhangwei's original plan was approved by the majority.

(3) (Note 6) The former University Council issued a survey form in 1928 to the education administrative authorities of various provinces and cities, detailing the number of school-age children. The original deadline for reporting was the end of 1928, but at that time, the Northern Expedition had just been successfully completed, and the military operations had not ended for long. Many provinces and cities delayed or did not handle the survey of school-age children. As of September 1929, only Nanjing Special City had reported the exact number of school-age children to the Ministry. The remaining provinces and cities did not report accurate figures. Therefore, the number of school-age children nationwide can only be estimated based on the approximate population of the country. In European and American countries, approximately one in six people is a school-age child, but the "school-age period" for children in China is temporarily set from six to twelve years old. If necessary, it can be extended to fifteen years old. The period is shorter than that of Europe and the United States, and compulsory education is also temporarily targeted at "enabling school-age children nationwide to receive four years of elementary school education." Therefore, the number can be further reduced. It is now tentatively assumed that one in ten people is a school-age child who should receive compulsory education.

Huang Jianzhong said that the amendment "(may be extended to fifteen years if necessary)" should not be added and should be deleted. Chen Jian said that the amendment to Note 6 conflicted with the original text of Note 2, so the original plan should be maintained. When it was put to a vote, the majority supported maintaining the original plan, which was passed. Speaker Jiang asked whether this case was passed as a whole. Meng Xiancheng said that issues related to teacher training had not yet been discussed, so it could not be considered to be passed as a whole. Zhu Jingnong proposed that this case should reserve the two points of teacher training funding budget, and the rest should be passed. When it was put to a vote, the majority supported Zhu Jingnong's proposal, which was passed. Zhang Honglie, Director of the Henan Education Department, Photo by Guanghua.

Academia Sinica Receives Members 100

▲ President Cai's Speech ▲ Jin Zecheng's Response

Academia Sinica hosted a reception for its members at 5:00 PM on the 17th, specially inviting all members to visit the Meteorological Observatory. The Secretary-General, Yang Xingfo, Secretary Xu Jifu, and staff of the Academy guided the visit. This is the old site of the Taipei Observatory, and the architecture is very grand, and the equipment is also plentiful. A library is now under construction behind the observatory and work has already begun. After the visit, they went to Jiming Temple. President Cai had already arrived and personally welcomed them. At 6:00 PM, a banquet was held at Huomeng Building. More than one hundred members attended, and guests included Wu Zhihui and Li Shishi. During the banquet, Cai gave a speech, briefly saying that it was a great pleasure to invite all teaching members here today. The relationship between Academia Sinica and education is very close. The Academy is in its initial stage, and the existing research institutes, such as meteorology, astronomy, geology, natural history, physics, chemistry, and industry, are mostly in the field of natural sciences. The number of social sciences is very small. There is currently only one social research institute, which is divided into legal, economic, and social groups. Because research institutes in practical subjects are relatively easy to establish, as long as there are a few researchers and some instruments, research can be carried out. The Academy is established by the state, and its nature is different from that of the university's research institute. The university's research institute is designed to train university graduates for more in-depth knowledge. The nature of the Academy is to allow scholars to have a free research opportunity according to their interests, and sometimes choose a few practical problems for research, providing reference for various social, political, and educational undertakings. The Academy originally had a plan to set up an educational research institute, because the scope of this research institute is very broad, and the talent, of course, cannot be done by a few people. In terms of equipment, it cannot be done with some instruments. A laboratory must have various experimental schools as its research place, and the required funding is also very large, so it cannot be started. Now the Ministry of Education has a plan to set up an educational research institute, hoping to cooperate with the Academy, and the Academy expresses its approval. I am very happy to have you here today. Please raise a glass of light wine to wish you good health and to wish the national education progress. Then, Jin Zecheng, the representative of Guangdong, was elected by the members to give a reply. Jin Jun once served as the Dean of the Former University Council and once worked with President Cai to plan the establishment of various research projects. The reply was very sincere, briefly saying: I am very grateful to President Cai for hosting colleagues today. We deeply know that President Cai advocated the establishment of Academia Sinica when he was at the University Council. When it was established, although there was no foundation, today, due to proper management, several research institutes have been established, and branches have been set up in Shanghai, Nanjing, and other places. This kind of academic construction is very common in Eastern and Western countries, but in China, it can be regarded as a new construction. I feel that Nanjing in the past few years and Nanjing today have made a lot of progress. For example, Beijige was dilapidated before, but now it has built an astronomical observatory, and other constructions are also numerous. Academia Sinica is an organization for scientific construction and academic construction and is closely related to the education sector. More than a dozen of China's education sectors have not seen progress, which is due to the lack of scientific and academic construction. Now the President is doing this matter, and there will be great construction in science and academics. Colleagues deeply hope that President Cai will expand this construction to other provinces, and colleagues will be very grateful. Colleagues also know that President Cai has a good capacity for alcohol, so please all gentlemen raise a glass together to wish President Cai good health.
