News of Sino-American Aviation Contract Conference 145

▲ The Representative Sent by the American Side is Not Qualified

▲ The Aviation Industry Plans to Request a Recall

Since the China Aviation Corporation signed a Sino-American aviation contract with the American Aviation Development Corporation in May last year, the China Aviation Association, the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, and aviation personnel in various places have all believed that the contract is greatly detrimental to the Chinese side and have actively opposed it. After Sun Ke, the chairman of the board of directors of the China Aviation Corporation, resigned, the National Government appointed Wang Boqun, the Minister of Communications, concurrently. Wang valued public opinion and carefully reviewed the contract with various departments and also believed that it needed to be revised or abolished. The National Government then ordered the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Communications, and the China Aviation Corporation to hold a meeting with the American representative to resolve the issue. Minister Wang notified the American Flying Transport Corporation to select a representative to come to Beijing to discuss all the details. According to news from the aviation industry yesterday, the representative sent by the American side, Max Apollin, is a businessman engaged in the kerosene business. He is not familiar with the aviation business and is not suitable to be a representative. This meeting may not have good results. Therefore, the aviation industry plans to submit a request to the authorities to consult with the United States to recall Apollin and send a qualified person so that the two parties can sign a mutually beneficial treaty and promote international transportation.

Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Industry and Commerce Provide Relief to 100,000 Rickshaw Pullers in Shanghai 146

▲ Chen Shiguang Visits Fessenden, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council

▲ Please Restore the Vehicles Recovered in 1924 Quickly

In 1924, the Public Concession Shanghai Municipal Council recovered 5,161 rickshaws with licenses. It was originally scheduled that after a five-year period, the vehicles would be returned as appropriate. Unexpectedly, after the expiration date at the end of August last year, the Municipal Council delayed the return on various pretexts, resulting in more than 100,000 unemployed workers in Shanghai. Wang Zhengting, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, attached great importance to this matter and ordered Chen Shiguang, the director of the Shanghai office, to quickly resolve the issue with the Concession authorities to provide relief to the poor and eliminate hidden dangers. At the same time, the Minister of Industry and Commerce also sent a special commissioner to Shanghai yesterday to contact all parties. The news obtained is divided as follows:

▲ Instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Chen Shiguang, the director of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, received instructions from the Ministry the day before yesterday, stating: According to the report from Shanghai merchants Zheng Limin and others, rickshaw workers in the Shanghai Public Concession are being forced into unemployment, which is inhumane. Following the order, I went to the Chinese and Foreign Rickshaw Merchants Association and the Rickshaw Workers' Mutual Aid Association to discuss the matter, but the two associations refused to discuss it. I have repeatedly requested the Municipal Government, but there is no relief plan. I can only submit photos of the tragic situation of fighting for rickshaws and request the British Consul to instruct the Municipal Council to issue the 5,161 rickshaw licenses recovered in 1924 to save lives. It is found that this matter was previously reported by the people, and it was instructed that the original approval of the Shanghai Special Municipal Government should be followed, and the Chinese and Foreign Rickshaw Merchants Association and the Rickshaw Workers' Mutual Aid Association should be consulted to apply for handling. If the two associations refuse to discuss, they should request the Municipal Government to review and decide on relief. Now, according to the report, it seems that the two associations may have obstructed the matter because they have separately recognized the vehicles donated to the Public Concession. Since there are more vehicles demanded than supplied, in order to provide relief to the poor and eliminate hidden dangers, a portion of the vehicle licenses recovered in 1924 should be issued immediately to resolve disputes and prevent any party from holding the licenses for a long time. Therefore, a copy of the report and six photos are issued, instructing the office to quickly negotiate with the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council to handle the matter appropriately and report back. This order.

▲ The Course of Events The reporter of the New Shanghai News Agency visited a certain official from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce who came to Shanghai at the inn and was informed of the course of events in great detail. It is reported that the Shanghai Public Concession rickshaw licenses totaled 15,161 due to the prosperity of the market. In 1924, the car dealers who donated the licenses manipulated and monopolized the business, fabricated reasons for traffic congestion, and requested the Municipal Council to recover 5,161 car licenses, resulting in more than 100,000 unemployed workers. However, when the Municipal Council recovered the car licenses, it stipulated a five-year period, at which time it would be restored as appropriate. Unexpectedly, after the expiration in August last year, the workers, compelled by starvation, elected representatives to request the Municipal Council and the Municipal Government to issue the recovered car licenses. At that time, the association still obstructed the matter. Although the petitioners exhausted their voices, the listeners remained deaf. The workers had no choice but to send representatives Zheng Limin and others to Beijing in January of this year to petition the Ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, and Industry and Commerce. Ministers Kong and Wang attached great importance to this matter. In recent years, dozens of counties in Jiangbei have suffered from continuous droughts, and the disaster is extremely severe, causing the people to suffer, families to be separated, and the poor to have difficulty maintaining their lives. They have had no choice but to come to Shanghai to pull rickshaws, and the number of workers has suddenly increased to more than 100,000, gathering in Shanghai, waiting expectantly for the issuance of the car licenses every day. If the car licenses are not issued for a day, they cannot live for a day. In case they are forced by starvation to take risks or incidents similar to the May 30th Massacre occur, the hidden dangers are unimaginable. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has ordered Director Chen to earnestly resolve the issue with the Concession authorities.

▲ Visiting Fessenden Director Chen Shiguang, after receiving the instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs the day before yesterday, decided to negotiate with the Concession authorities yesterday. In the morning, a certain gentleman from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce came to Shanghai from Beijing and went to the office at Fenglin Bridge to discuss the matter with Chen for a long time. All kinds of methods were discussed in detail. Chen then visited Fessenden, the chairman of the Municipal Council, in the afternoon for an informal contact and sent letters to the General Affairs and European and American divisions of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The results of the negotiations will be reported at any time.

The Problem of the Silk and Satin Industry Organizing a Trade Association 148

▲ Gradually Approaching

The dispute between the various silk and satin guilds in this city against the consolidation and reorganization of the Trade Association by the Chamber of Commerce has been going on for a long time. The focus of the dispute is that the Chamber of Commerce, according to Article 5 of the Trade Association Law, which states that there should be only one Trade Association in a region, insists on the merger. The various guilds argue that the organizational situation of each guild is different and that they have their own historical relationship, so they advocate separate establishment. It is now reported that the Social Affairs Bureau specially convened a discussion meeting on the afternoon of the 14th of this month to collect opinions in order to resolve the issue. The representatives present on that day included Tao Baichuan from the City Party Headquarters, Lu Youshao from the Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Yansong, Jiang Linshu, Luo Qinghua, Lu Zhengbing, and more than ten others from the Silk and Satin Industry Organizing Committee. Director Pan of the Social Affairs Bureau presided over the meeting and explained the legal principles and facts in detail. After three hours of discussion, the opinions of all parties on the merger and reorganization have gradually become consistent. They still respect the laws and regulations and organize a unified organization. However, it is proposed to stipulate in the charter of the Trade Association that the original guilds should be divided into groups, such as the Huzhou crepe group and the Suzhou satin group, which will be responsible for studying various issues related to the group, increasing the partial interests of the group, and keeping the original property of the group. In order to avoid difficulties in implementation in terms of facts, this method can take care of both laws and facts. The representatives of the various guilds are also satisfied. The Social Affairs Bureau immediately sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce the next day to inform them of the results of the meeting in the hope that this dispute would be resolved as soon as possible.

The Zhabei Industry Association Still Asks to be Reorganized 149

The Zhabei Industry Association sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: We have received your letter No. 973, which opened on April 10th, stating: We have received a letter from the Shanghai Special City Social Affairs Bureau, which opened on April 7th (as seen in the previous report, omitted). We have found that our association prepared the procedures in accordance with the Trade Association Organization Law on May 15, 1929, and submitted them to the Shanghai Special City Social Affairs Bureau for registration. The application was approved because the members of our association included foreign merchants, and registration was not allowed. Later, on July 26 of the same year, our association reorganized and improved, and on August 7 of the same year, we prepared the procedures and sent a letter to your association requesting approval for registration. A license No. 80 was issued. We have found that the business of building and leasing operated by the members of our association is affirmed by the general manager as the most important enterprise, and the mayor’s approval No. 1196 also confirms that our industry is a kind of business. There is no doubt that our association is a legitimate commercial organization. As for saying that the interests of property owners have been legally guaranteed, the same is true for other industries. The organization of the Trade Association is for the purpose of increasing the knowledge of the industry and seeking the construction of the industry together, not for the purpose of requesting the protection of legal interests. It is even more difficult to admit that our association is a disguised form of the homeowners association and is the basis for not allowing registration. Our industry is engaged in real estate, and other merchants are engaged in the transaction of goods. The matter is the same, so our association's application for registration is completely a legitimate act of good citizens. However, we have repeatedly applied and have not been approved. We are very embarrassed. Your association leads business operations and unifies organizations, and should not allow the real estate industry to be left out. We hereby reiterate our previous request and ask you to forward a letter to the Shanghai Special City Social Affairs Bureau, requesting that our association be reorganized in accordance with the law. This is for the public good. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Special City Merchant Group Organizing Committee.

Wusong Fishing Season is Approaching 153

▲ The Outer Bund is Densely Populated

▲ The Anti-Smuggling Team Arranges in Advance

The Wusong spring fish market occupies the commercial center of the whole town. Every year after Qingming Festival, when the spring fish season is approaching, the three fish shops, Qiancui, Baofeng, and Shenthai, all go to Wusong to make arrangements, wait for the fish boats to enter the port, and then start business. Others, such as men, women, old and young from Shandong Tao and Yancheng, are familiar with the boat owners and rely on the fish rafts (commonly known as "chasing the foreign rafts") to make a living, and have been coming to Wusong one after another in recent days, either living on boats or renting houses temporarily, in order to earn a living. As a result, the Outer Bund area has become densely populated in recent days, and the market is more prosperous. There are also various agencies related to the fishing rafts, such as the water police anti-smuggling camp, who are planning various plans for protecting and arresting smuggled salt. Yesterday, the first brigade of the anti-smuggling team stationed in Wusong issued a notice, which is copied as follows: Notice from the First Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Department of the Salt Affairs of the Five Districts of Jiangsu: For the purpose of notice, it is known that the jurisdiction of this brigade is vast and adjacent to the sea. Every fishing raft is related to the smooth flow of the official sales of the five districts of Jiangsu. The fishing raft season of this year is approaching, and arrangements should be made in advance. The Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Songhu Garrison Command have been requested to issue announcements and regulations separately for notification. All fishers and fish merchants should be informed and complied with. Fishing boats must abide by the ban, and fish merchants must not collude. If they violate the rules, they will be punished according to the regulations. The officers and soldiers of this brigade must also be diligent and cautious in their duties and abide by the scope. Local ruffians and hooligans must not take advantage of the fishing raft season to rely on the crowd to rob salt brine and cause trouble, resulting in being caught by the law. If there are unscrupulous people who cause trouble on the pretext of the fishing rafts, they are allowed to report to the department for strict handling. The brigade commander will enforce the law strictly and will not be lenient. Each should comply strictly. This notice. Brigade Commander Wu Shuzi.

Zhabei Japanese Residents' House Tax Issue 155

▲ Xu Zhizhi, Tang Zhenchao, Confer with Japanese Residents' Representatives

Xu Zhizhi, also known as Jinshang, the director of the Shanghai Special Municipality Finance Bureau's North City Tax Collection Office, hails from Dongshan, Dongting Lake, and has resided in the North City for a long time. He is well-versed in local conditions. Since last year, he was appointed by Director Xu upon a request to Mayor Zhang to handle tax collection matters in the North City. Because some Japanese residents were unwilling to acknowledge and pay the tax, he was eager to negotiate, compelling them to comply and pay uniformly. Therefore, he requested Director Xu to appoint Tang Zhenchao, who is familiar with the situation of Japanese residents and proficient in Japanese, as an investigator of overseas merchants. Recently, Director Xu, accompanied by Investigator Tang, made an appointment with Japanese leaders (Chairman of the Shanghai Japanese Roads Federation) Lin Xionggji, (Member) Kobayashi Kaname, (Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai Japanese Roads Federation) Kondo Mitsuru, and (Chairman of the Shanghai Japanese Residents' Conference) Ohtsuki Shigeru, at No. 69 Wenlu Road to hold a discussion. After meeting, they exchanged business cards and took their seats. Director Xu spoke first, saying, "I have come here today to visit regarding the collection of house tax in the North City, which is under my responsibility. Some of your country's residents have paid, while many have not. There may be some misunderstandings, so I have come specifically to explain. In the past, it was called 'general tax,' with residents paying 6% and businesses paying 10%. Although it was called 'general tax,' there were still many other taxes, such as security and fire protection. Not only did your country's residents find it troublesome, but so did our own citizens. Therefore, the municipal government decided at a meeting in the 18th year of the Republic [1929] to cancel all other items and change it to house tax, with residents paying 10% and businesses paying 14%, split equally between landlord and tenant. The tenants pay on behalf of the landlords and deduct it when paying rent. The residents may have misunderstood due to the sudden increase in the tax rate, not knowing that the house tax is split equally between landlord and tenant. For residents, the 10% is actually only 5%, and for businesses, the 14% is actually only 7%, which is actually less than the old 'general tax.' Also, I saw on your association's leaflets that although the landlord and tenant are nominally each paying half, the landlord can easily increase the rent, resulting in the tenant bearing the entire burden. I am unaware that the municipal government has previously rejected a request from the tenants' association to not allow rent increases. Whether or not an increase should be made should be agreed upon by both landlord and tenant for it to take effect. The residents also mistakenly believe that paying tax on behalf of the landlord is a misunderstanding." Lin Xionggji, Kondo Mitsuru, and Ohtsuki Shigeru then spoke, saying, "Director Xu's visit today to explain the various points has certainly clarified some misunderstandings." They then asked, "Are the taxes graded?" Director Xu replied, "Yes, they are divided into housing and shops. Housing is 10%, meaning one yuan per month for every ten yuan of rent, collected quarterly at three yuan, split equally between landlord and tenant. Shops are 14%, calculated in the same manner." They asked, "Can the director collect the landlord's share directly to avoid the landlord refusing to acknowledge payment, causing the tenant to be oppressed by both sides?" Director Xu replied, "The city government's regulations seem difficult to change. If the landlord refuses to acknowledge it, it is a violation of the tax rate, and the city government will have a way to deal with it. Besides, how could a landlord be willing to forfeit a large amount of rent for the sake of a small amount of tax?" The gentlemen also said, "The house tax issue has been unresolved for several years since Ding Wenjiang's negotiations in 1926. Now that Director Xu has come here, both sides can explain the various points. We will persuade the residents to pay the tax according to regulations. However, it would still be best if the director collected the landlord's share directly to avoid complications. Special attention should also be paid to hygiene and police matters." The conversation lasted for three hours. The gentlemen invited Director Xu and Tang to lunch at the club, and the host and guests parted on amicable terms.

Disaster Survey Diary of the Xinghua Branch of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association 158

Lu Henry, the Western Chairman of the Xinghua Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, and Hong Youxin, the Chinese Chairman, reported in person to the Shanghai Association the day before yesterday, saying, "What we have witnessed during this survey is a particularly tragic disaster situation. Moreover, as spring has just begun, all grain seeds have been exhausted, and there are no resources for cultivation. Even in the eastern countryside, although there are wheat fields, most have been sown but have not sprouted. Those that have sprouted are also suffering from insect pests and will soon wither. In this situation, the victims are in dire straits and can barely survive. Their lives have no hope. If we do not cry out for relief, watching hundreds of thousands of victims suffer the same great catastrophe, we are not made of iron and stone, how can we bear it? Furthermore, if they cannot find food, they will inevitably resort to desperate measures. The world is in turmoil, and hidden worries will never end. The urgency of spring relief is ten times greater than winter relief." They also presented handwritten diaries, recorded as follows: "We five personally went to the countryside to inspect the disaster situation and made a brief report. On the first day, from Xinghua to Cha'an, Tangzi Town, and Xin Town, we saw very few wheat fields, and the farmers were extremely distressed. We also went to Supilin, Tantan, Xinzhuang, and Heta Weirs. These places have always relied entirely on wheat fields for their livelihood. This year, due to fleeing outwards, the fields have been left barren. In Xinzhuang Weir, we saw a woman surnamed Wu with six children who had not eaten for three days and wanted to commit suicide. Fortunately, they immediately received more than a peck of wheat bran, saving her family's life. On the second day, we braved the rain to go to Baiju to see the porridge factory. More than a thousand hungry people had already come, waiting for porridge to eat. Most had traveled from more than fifteen miles away, all with yellow faces and thin skin. We took five photos. Afterwards, we went to the east side of Lao Weir to inspect. The disaster was particularly severe, and there had been no harvest for two years. Everything was barren. Even if there was wheat, it had already withered, and there were also earthworms in the fields, damaging the wheat roots. It was truly a human tragedy. We also saw Zhanglin, Wanzhuang, and Zhu Peng's three villages. They had already run out of food and were eating grass roots and tree bark to survive. The Central Weir in the fifth district was even more miserable than Lao Weir. On the third day, we went to Anfeng to see the porridge factory. More than a thousand victims had already come, begging for food from the porridge cook. The situation was very distressing. We specially took several photos. We also went to Daying and saw that the victims receiving porridge were all coming by boat from afar. Dozens of people in each boat, braving the rain and enduring hunger, were shivering all over, which was even more miserable. We returned to Yongfeng Weir and other places. Six out of ten families had sealed their doors with mud and fled to various places in Jiangnan to escape the famine. The remaining victims were all eating grass roots and wild vegetables. Chickens and dogs had long disappeared, and the fields were all dry and barren. All the victims were so hungry that they had only bones and no flesh, which made people weep. The disaster situation was so severe that we have reported it accordingly." It is heard that the Shanghai Association has allocated six thousand yuan, which is only a drop in the bucket. They are currently seeking assistance from all walks of life.

Daughter-in-law Sold to Opium Den 161

▲ Both Defendants Evasive

Chen Shiliang, a Jiangbei native of Hujia Wood Bridge, Linping Road, North Shanghai, had a daughter-in-law raised from childhood, Xiao Yuzi, aged fifteen. On March 12th of this year, at 5:00 PM, she disappeared after finishing work at the factory and returning home. Chen searched repeatedly without success. Later, neighbors Liu Wansong and Zhou San also disappeared at the same time, leading to great suspicion. Now that these people have suddenly reappeared, Chen believes that there are clues to be found from Liu, Zhou, and others. He reported to the police, and they were detained in the Third Precinct of the Fifth District. According to Chen Shiliang's statement, the defendants confessed to luring his daughter-in-law to Zhenjiang first, but there were no customers. They then returned to Shanghai and sold her to an opium den behind the Great World for 140 yuan. When questioned, the defendants were evasive. They were all sent to the local court for questioning.

Bu Rong, Mentally Disturbed, Throws Himself into Huangpu River 162

▲ Devouring Banknotes

The Taikoo Company's Suiyang steamship, coming from Xiamen to Shanghai, was passing the Gaoqiao wharf when one of the passenger soldiers suddenly walked to the deck and jumped into the river. Fortunately, Shi Haichun and others who were receiving guests at the New Inn saw him and immediately tried to rescue him, allowing him to regain his life. He was then sent to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team yesterday afternoon at around 4:00 PM to be placed. After preliminary interrogation by Captain Xu, he stated his name was Bu Rong, 33 years old, from Hunan. He was a clerk in the Second Battalion of the 46th Regiment of the Eighth Division of the National Revolutionary Army. Recently, he received a letter from home, learning that his elderly father had passed away. He immediately asked for leave and boarded the Suiyang steamship to Shanghai, preparing to transfer to another ship to return to Hunan. Unexpectedly, on the Suiyang steamship, several stragglers suddenly robbed him of all the 42 yuan he had with him and tried to harm him. He was so frightened that he had no choice but to throw himself into the river to commit suicide. Later, Qu Wuqiao, the company commander of the Artillery Battalion of the 50th Division of the National Revolutionary Army, reported to the team that Bu Rong had recently suffered from mental illness, causing him to be mentally disturbed. When he was on the steamship, he threw teapots, teacups, and other items, and put the banknotes he had with him into his mouth and chewed them wildly. Therefore, under his witness, he took his funds for safekeeping. His luggage is now stored in the Taian Hotel. Please verify. Seeing Bu Rong's attitude, the captain thought that he seemed to be suffering from a mental illness and immediately sent police to the Taian Hotel to retrieve his luggage, along with all his funds, and submitted a report to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for disposal.

Robbery in Qianjia Lane, West Shanghai 163

The home of Xue Genlin at No. 12 Qianjia Lane, Yanjiadian, Difeng Road, West Shanghai, was suddenly visited by three or four robbers yesterday morning at around 3:00 AM. They opened the door with a matching key and entered. Everyone was asleep. The robbers did not make a sound and immediately ransacked the chests and cabinets, searching for dozens of pieces of clothing, which they packed into two large packages. Just as the robbers were about to escape with the stolen goods, everyone woke up and noticed, getting up. The robbers became menacing, holding pistols to scare them into silence. They fled one after another with the stolen goods, which is what is called "soft entry, hard exit." Afterwards, the victims, Xue Genlin and Zhao Juting, filed a report with the Sixth District Police Station, requesting the pursuit of the stolen goods and robbers. It is said that the loss was over 600 yuan.

He then used force, assaulting two Indian constables, and was then taken to the patrol room. The defendant stated that he was 21 years old and currently residing in Shanghai, and admitted to his actions. The questioning official sentenced the defendant to seven days in prison and required a guarantor to ensure his future good behavior. If he could not find a guarantor, he would be deported back to India.

Emergency Meeting of Tenement Residents in Zhen'an Lane Yesterday 168

The case of the tenement residents of Zhen'an Lane, Ximen Road, French Concession, where the landlord cut off the water supply and forcibly erected bamboo fences under the pretext of rebuilding houses, causing a conflict, has been ongoing for many days. Fearing further oppression by the landlord, the residents held a temporary emergency meeting at No. 10 of the lane yesterday afternoon at 8:00 PM to prevent such incidents. All residents, except for two, were present, totaling over one hundred people. General Representative Ge Fulong was elected chairman. After the report, they discussed the matter together. General Representative Li Shuangyu spoke about the facts of the losses, and Representatives Zheng Dun, Sun Linfu, Wu Zhangshi, and Shen Lishi all applauded and agreed. The chairman put it to a vote, and everyone rejected the landlord's behavior and declared that the residents' purpose was to seek housing, not money. Next, they discussed methods of seeking external assistance and resolved to issue a declaration in the name of the Housing Association and to inform all citizens of the illegal oppression and the suffering of the residents. Finally, the chairman reported that according to the Municipal Party Headquarters, they had sent staff to secretly investigate the details of the case and that the Municipal Housing Association had sent a letter. The discussion on financial issues was enthusiastic, and the meeting adjourned at 12:00 AM.

The Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association sent a letter to Mr. Fevrier of the French General Patrol Room yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, we have found that landlords in the French Concession often evict tenants, using coercive means such as surrounding them with bamboo fences, and colluding with water and electricity workers to cut off water and electricity. We have also found police officers present at the scene to help them. The industrial and police organs were originally established to protect the local area and maintain law and order and should not be controlled by the landlord. Moreover, violating public opinion for private interests is even more intolerable by law. The association's responsibility lies in this, and it is difficult to stand idly by. If it is not immediately corrected, the disturbances will inevitably worsen. Therefore, we have attached a petition from the Zhen'an Lane Residents' Association and respectfully ask that you, as the general supervisor, consider the will of the people, strictly prohibit such behavior, and provide a reply to reassure the public."

Business Report of American Asiatic Life Insurance Company 171

The American Asiatic Life Insurance Company held a shareholders' meeting the day before yesterday. General Manager Mr. Steere reported on the business situation for the year 1929, stating briefly that the company's effective insurance amount has now increased to 6,830,930 yuan, with a total amount reaching 24,098,486 yuan. The company's assets have increased to 1,452,198 yuan and 94 cents, the reserve has increased by 493,539 yuan and 31 cents, and the net surplus is 54,709 yuan and 02 cents. In 1929, the amount paid to policyholders and their parents, wives, and children reached 207,826 yuan and 24 cents. The mortality rate in China is recently considered exceptionally good. In the company's past nine years of history, the mortality rate in Shanghai has been lower than the ordinary standard in the United States. Southern China also has exceptional records. In China, only two places, Fuzhou and Hankou, have higher mortality rates than usual. The mortality rate in the Philippines is higher than the average, but the company has not been operating there for long, and our experience cannot be used to draw conclusions. The mortality rate in French Annam is very good, but it cannot be taken as a definite conclusion, as the operating period is only two years. The company's business area expanded to Java, the Malay Archipelago, and the South Sea Islands in 1929. However, operations in the Kingdom of Luo Luo have been suspended because the local courts cannot protect life insurance companies in cases of fraudulent claims. In one case, even though there was insufficient evidence of the policyholder's death, the court ruled that the company should pay compensation. Several months later, the company discovered the policyholder who falsely claimed to be dead, and handed him over to the police station. This person may still be in prison, but the insurance money paid by the company has not yet been recovered. In another case, even though the company had a certificate from the Ministry of Interior of the local government proving that there was no evidence of the policyholder's death, it still had to pay compensation. Although the political situation in China has been constantly turbulent in recent years, the life insurance business has become an economic organization of the country and is gradually progressing. The company's board of directors firmly believes that this situation is of great benefit to the future of American Asiatic operations. Last year, an independent division was established, specializing in the sale of accidental injury and health insurance, under the leadership of Mr. Gao Luosen. The ability of this division to work has led to the company's plan to realize its independent organization in the near future, so that it can specialize in managing American Asiatic's accident and health insurance.

Free Talk

A Smile 176

— Sea Guest

▲Father: Child, if you are so naughty, I must spank you. Your mother also agrees.

Child: Father, you are so pitiful. Is this the only thing your mother agrees with you on?

▲A: Why are athletes not allowed to sell gold medals, silver tripods, silver cups, and other prizes they win?

B: I'm afraid they'll estimate their prices.

▲Female: God created man first, and then created woman.

Male: So women often follow behind men, asking for this today and that tomorrow, entangled for life.

▲A: Do you feel tired when you talk so eloquently?

B: Chatting with old friends is the happiest thing, and I don't feel tired at all.

A: I'm very sorry, but my ear is tired of listening. Let me switch to the other ear to listen.

▲Female: When you proposed to me last night, did you expect that I would agree to you immediately?

Male: I expected it long ago, because I came feeling scared, as if something bad was going to happen.

▲Male: Dear, you are the bright moon in my eyes and the sunshine in my life. When you are by my side, you can resist all storms.

Female: Are you telling me about love, or are you making an astronomical observatory report?

Welcoming President Chiang's Visit 177

— Jian Nong from Xuzhou

The situation of Chairman Chiang's visit to Xuzhou has been detailed in various newspapers. However, there are still anecdotes and scattered news that were not recorded by various newspapers. I have selected them and recorded them. It is also a good story of welcoming Chiang.

▲Mourning at the Martyrs' Cemetery The Martyrs' Cemetery at the foot of Yunlong Mountain in the south of the city is where the remains of the martyrs of the First Army of the Northern Expedition are placed. It was built in the winter of the 17th year and rebuilt in the summer of the 18th year. It has recently been expanded to bury the fallen soldiers of the First Division in successive campaigns against the rebels. It is already under construction. Chairman Chiang, after getting off the car in the early morning, summoned the generals at the Second Route Headquarters and then took a car to the cemetery to mourn. Those who accompanied him were Liu Zhi, Gu Zhutong, Han Fuqu, Ma Hongkui, He Yaogzu, Chen Jicheng, and Xu Tingyao and other important generals. At that time, the reporters sent telegrams to the Second Route Headquarters, the railway station, No. 1 Room of the Longhai Road, and Jiulishan, but they did not find the whereabouts of the chairman. Therefore, there was no such news in the newspapers, which is a great pity.

▲Summoning the Children Chairman Chiang once visited Yunlong Mountain during the Northern Expedition in the past. He met a young child, Zhang Shaoxin, of a photographer and loved him very much. He called him a little friend. He once took him to the General Headquarters to play. Later, whenever he came to Xuzhou, he would summon him whenever he had time. This time, when he arrived at the Martyrs' Cemetery, he remembered the little friend again. He sent someone to summon him. Chiang stood on the altar of the cemetery and said to him, "Little friend, I haven't seen you for more than a year." Zhang replied, "I haven't seen the Chairman for more than a year. Now it's the third Northern Expedition." Chiang also asked Zhang what his family did now. Zhang replied that he was taking pictures in the mountain. When Chiang heard this, he said, "Very good. Let's take pictures." So the Chairman and the generals went to Yunlong Mountain to take a photo. Zhang carried the camera for his father. Chiang praised him very much. I visited Yunlong Mountain yesterday and went to Zhang's Jiyun Photo Studio. I asked Zhang Shaoxin what he said and saw the group photo of Chiang and the generals. It is not a fiction. Zhang is 15 years old this year and is studying at Hubushan Elementary School.

▲Photography of Yunlong Mountain After Chiang visited the Martyrs' Cemetery, he took photos with the generals on the west slope of Yunlong Mountain. Chiang wore a black cloak. Those who took photos with him were Han Fuqu, Liu Zhi, Ma Hongkui, He Yaogzu, Gu Zhutong, Chen Jicheng, Xu Tingyao, etc. There is the three-character inscription "Yunlong Mountain" written by Mo Yuqi, the right counselor of Xuzhou Military Preparation in the 14th year of Wanli of the Ming Dynasty. There is also the inscription written by Mr. Dai Jitao when he visited Xuzhou last year. The stone wall has been chiseled and is still waiting to be published. (Payment required)

Common Sense Gleanings 178

— Ma Zuqian

When sitting in a train car and looking out the window, never face the front of the train, because the coal smoke will blow into your eyes.

▲In the third- or fourth-class cabins of Yangtze River steamers or trains, people often walk around and shout, "Beware of hairy hands." You must not use your hands to touch your body to see if your money is still there, otherwise you will be deceived. Knowing where your money is makes it easier to steal.

▲Eyeglasses must be wiped and placed properly so that no scratches appear on the glass surface. Otherwise, not only will they not help your eyesight, but they will also cause headaches and dizziness from time to time.

▲When using a towel in a public place such as a bathhouse or tavern to wipe your face, you must close your eyes tightly, lest there be淋菌 on it, which can cause blindness or other eye diseases, which are enough to harm your eye health.

▲Clenching your teeth every time you urinate can prevent your teeth from falling out for life. They will be firm and free from disease. Books have also said this. I saw an 81-year-old man in Shanghai who could eat peanuts. He said he used this method. Fortunately, it doesn't cost much. Why don't everyone do this? Getting healthy teeth is a kind of happiness.

(Unpaid)

Grave Talk 179

— Qing Qu

Regarding graves, Shuowen says, "Mounds." Zheng Sinong said that it is the land of tombs, a place for filial sons to remember. Therefore, it is called a grave. In the Zhouli Chun Guan, the grave minister is in charge. He makes a map of the territory of all the graves in the country and orders the people to be buried there. He listens to the lawsuits for those who fight for the grave land. He leads his subordinates to patrol the graves. It is said that the graves are limited to the concealed places. Commoners do not seal or plant trees. Therefore, it is not called a mound but a grave. Yangzi Fangyan says, "All burials without mounds are called graves, and burials with mounds are called graves." Therefore, Tanjing says, "A grave without a mound." Also, a flat grave is called a mound, and a high one is called a grave. However, it is also said that the ancients did not repair graves. Easy graves are not ancient. Their system is different from the current mixed use of the word "grave."

The common saying is "hanging the grave," but it is not known when it started. In the Spring and Autumn period, Yanling Jizi passed by the lord of Xu in the north. The lord of Xu liked Jizi's sword but dared not say it. Jizi knew it in his heart. He was sent to the upper country and did not offer it. When he returned to Xu, the lord of Xu had already died. Therefore, he took off the sword and tied it to the tree of the lord of Xu's tomb and left. His followers said, "The lord of Xu is dead, who should I give it to?" Jizi said, "No, I promised it in my heart. How can I betray my heart because of death?" This is recorded in the Longmen Historical Records. It is said to be "hanging the sword." Today, people call it "hanging the grave." It has a source, but its meaning is not.

Some say it is "sweeping the grave," not "hanging the grave." However, the Wu people read the sound of "grave" like "wu," which is the same as the "mu" of farmland, and they do not pronounce the correct sound. As for those who hang paper money on the grave, this thing is also called "grave" sound, but they say "wu." When people hear it suddenly, they almost don't understand what it means. It is really laughable. In the past, people took pride in obtaining the graves of their ancestors, but those who had a comprehensive view said that the person was dead and his ghost was not working. Has anyone ever seen wine and meat carried into the Nine Springs? A Song poem says, "Paper ashes fly like white butterflies, tears and blood dye red azaleas." It also says, "Who knows who is wise or foolish after a thousand years? The eyes are full of artemisia and they share a mound." It can also be said that he has spoken enough.

At this time of the Qingming Festival, stepping out of the city gate for a few steps, one can often see people wandering among the withered grass and barren land. Before long, a pig's trotter and several lines of wine are offered. The widows and weak concubines worship and offer. The smell of wine and meat fills the fields. The sound of crying is sad, corresponding to the sound of the pine trees. Looking at those beside them, they also sigh with emotion. However, this is the so-called green tomb. Although the person is dead, his bones have not yet cooled. If he lived in a splendid house, he would fall and return to the mountains and hills. The shepherd boys and woodcutters cut down the grave trees as firewood. The cunning rabbits and plump foxes dig up the grave fields to compete for holes. Even if there are broken steles and broken monuments, they fall by the roadside, and no one knows their surnames. Moreover, the barren tombs are piled up, and they are full of sight. And those who can not point to the grave door and sigh are few and far between. Thirty years ago, my country had a problem with being full of people. Some say there is no worry, but the worry is that the ghosts are full. Ghosts are full, which refers to the graveyard. Now I think it is true.

Random Notes on Wandering in America at the Zhuiyu Xuan 180

— Lai

Wanhua's visit to the United States this time received unparalleled welcome, and to receive unparalleled welcome with pure old Chinese drama was even more unexpected. There are indeed those who are experts in the field and study with their hearts here. I have already recorded the criticisms of Mr. Yang (a famous American writer), Stark Young. Now I will record his recent talks as follows.

In the second appearance of Fenhe Bay, he used his hands to sweep the dustpan. When the Chinese looked at the lost Xue Mu, he only swept it once in the first performance. After that, he swept it two or three times in a row, which was not as beautiful as the first time. (According to what was said in the first time, it was a body movement in the play, and what was done later was closer to the realistic school, so it is said that Mr. Yang is an expert.) Because the male lead is not very good, Mr. Mei reduced the highlights. If he had a good supporting role, Mr. Mei would be several times better. I think Mr. Mei's performance in China will be better than this. Performing here seems to be accommodating the Americans. I advise Mr. Mei not to do this, so as not to damage the value of Chinese drama. Those who come to see Mr. Mei's drama this time all view it from a very noble artistic point of view, or from an ancient sculpture point of view. Therefore, if there are places that they don't understand, it is not a hindrance at all. The more it is performed according to the old Chinese drama style, the more welcome and interested everyone is. Chinese drama is graceful and elegant, and its high position and heavy weight are the crown of world drama. I have learned a lot about the principles of drama and the principles of world art from watching Mr. Mei's this time. It is really very pleasant. I think Mr. Mei's voice is very good, but he seems to be afraid to sing hard. In fact, it doesn't matter. Now that New Yorkers have recognized Chinese drama as a world art, Mr. Mei should do his best to develop the inherent strengths of China. The more you develop, the more welcome you will be, because everyone is not here for entertainment, but for research. It is to study Eastern art. Therefore, Mr. Mei must not be discouraged, so as not to damage the value of Mr. Mei's art and the status of Chinese drama. Every few years in the United States, there will be a "Duo Jin Biao," which refers to people who are watched by the whole country. People from all walks of life, whether political or academic, are all in it. The "Duo Jin Biao" in recent years is Mr. Mei.

The above is the general idea of what Mr. Yang discussed. Mr. Yang's expertise is really convincing. Whenever Wanhua makes a slight change in the play, he will know it. Therefore, Wan is also very careful. Each time, there must be a certain place, otherwise someone will ask questions. Mr. Yang also said that the self-immolation of the tiger in the first performance was much better than the later ones. It can be seen that the audience is attentive.

A Record of Li Jilui 181

— Ji Gong

Li Jilui, an old man of literature and martial arts, is over sixty years old, and he is as healthy as ever. He has been away from the stage for ten years. This time, Chang Yunheng of the Shanghai stage made a special trip to the north to recruit him with courtesy, and it was difficult to refuse his kindness. He had no choice but to go south alone. Therefore, he returned to the stage, and it was a pleasant surprise to see him again on the red carpet with the folks in Chun Shen.

Li's fame was far away forty years ago. In the early years of the Republic of China, he enjoyed great fame in Beijing and Tianjin. He once came to Shanghai to perform for a month at the invitation of a certain stage. I once listened to his dramas such as "Falling Horse Lake" and "The Chain Set," and I was amazed. This time, I did not expect to meet him again. In recent days, I have also enjoyed his masterpieces such as "The Storm Pavilion," "Nine Righteous Men and Eighteen Heroes," and "Crouching Tiger Ridge." He is full of energy and his steps are from the guest. Looking at him is like a man in his thirties, and his style is not reduced at that time, but his subtlety is even better. His magnificent voice is beyond the reach of other actors. Looking at his meticulous expression and his crisp speech, it is as if he is meeting with ancient heroes. It can't help but make people feel lofty and courageous. When he plays Yue Wang in "The Storm Pavilion," his loyalty and righteousness are like a flash of lightning. His understanding is unique. It can be known that the success of art cannot be expected by luck or chance.

The drama "Hong Bi Yuan" is adapted from the novel "Green Peony." Li once compiled it into this drama and performed it in Beijing and Tianjin. Later, Lu Yueqiao directed it in the Chun Shen River. For a time, the audience praised it and the box office was unprecedented. This time, Li has agreed to write and arrange it. He will soon meet the audience. It is also good news for those who are fond of Zhou Lang. Mr. Sun Juxian, an old fellow villager, heard that he would arrive around the age of twenty or join the stage before Li's departure. Sun is ninety years old this year. It is said that his singing and chanting are still like in the past, but his ears are slightly deaf. However, with the proper accompaniment of the Huqin, there will be no mistakes. At that time, two old men of ninety-six and one hundred and fifty years old will work together, which is also a new record in the Shanghai theater industry.

Warmth in the Heart (173) 182

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Crimson Flames Soar, Theater Praises Filial Daughter; Red Carpet Lies Flat, Meeting Famous Actor Ah Jin on the Spot. "Never mind him. You said someone almost burned to death. Are you talking about the old woman?" A Bao said, "Of course. At that time, Miss Wen Guizhi the Third had just finished her stage performance. Many people upstairs all ran down. Everyone didn't know how the fire started. Luckily, the people in the theater sleep late. Everyone hadn't gone to bed yet. If it had been in the middle of the night, it would have been terrible. At this moment, everyone was accounted for, except for that old woman, who hadn't come downstairs yet. Miss Wen Guizhi the Third said, 'Oh no, that's terrible! Good Grandma hasn't come down. She's partially paralyzed. She has some hemiplegic problems. What can we do?' Looking at the handrail, it was filled with smoke, and even the electric lights couldn't be seen clearly. Then the Third Miss desperately rushed upstairs, shouting 'Good Grandma, Good Grandma, my Good Grandma.' Everyone saw her rushing upstairs and felt it was very dangerous, so they went to pull her back. Strangely, at this moment, she didn't know where she got the strength from. On ordinary days, she was so delicate that she seemed like she could be blown over by the wind. At this moment, her strength was extraordinary. No one could stop her. She said, 'The handrail hasn't been burned through yet, so it's okay. She lives very close to the handrail. If I grab her, I can drag her down, because the fire started very close to the handrail. If the handrail is burned through, it will be difficult.' At this moment, she rushed onto the handrail. Many people were sweating for her, shouting, 'Third Miss, come down quickly! Third Miss, come down quickly!' Her grandmother was originally suffering from paralysis. Now she couldn't stand such a fright. She was so frightened that she couldn't walk a step. That old woman also happened to be a big, heavy person. The Third Miss didn't care about anything. She carried her grandmother on her back, regardless of the consequences. The two of them reached the handrail, like rolling gourds. The two of them rolled down. We thought they must have been injured, but fortunately, they were not injured. In short, if the old woman didn't have this good granddaughter, she would have certainly been burned to death today. Everyone said that Miss Wen Guizhi the Third was truly filial, risking her life to save her grandmother. Just three minutes later, the handrail was burned through. Don't you think it was dangerous?" Ah Jin said, "It really was dangerous. If it were another young lady, she would have saved her own life. How could she have been willing to take this risk to save her grandmother? Did Wen Guizhi manage to salvage any of her jewelry or clothes?" A Bao said, "Apart from the jewelry she was wearing on her head and arms, because she had just finished her stage performance and hadn't taken them off, the rest in the room were all burned. It goes without saying about the clothes. There was no time to salvage the clothing chests. But Wen Guizhi didn't care at all. She said that clothes and jewelry were external things. If they were burned, she could buy them again in the future. As long as she saved her good grandma, she would be satisfied."

Cotton Yarn: Yarn Market in a Stalemate Between Bulls and Bears 192

The yarn market is flat and sluggish, trending soft due to poor actual sales and rumors of political instability, weakening sentiment. The market lacks excitement. Although buyers are not letting go, short sellers are heavily scouring the market for spot yarn, preparing to deliver against standard contracts. Therefore, the situation is still in flux. Bulls and bears are fiercely competing, making it difficult to predict the current situation. After closing, Dafeng Firm took in 1,000 bales of Honghefeng (Red Lotus Bee) 10-count yarn, reportedly also for delivery to the exchange.

Grains: River Rice Market Steadily Firm 195

▲ Zhabei: Yesterday, over ten sources from various gangs on the "Inside the Barriers" [i.e., Chinese-controlled areas of Shanghai] were selling well. Transactions in Gao Bai Jing [High Grade White Japonica Rice] from the Northern Gang were stagnant, and prices were flat. Medium and Lower grades of various Japonica rices from this area were selling more actively, but mainly in small quantities. Prices were steadily firming. Currently, stocks in the river [i.e., Yangtze River Delta region] are gradually decreasing. A few merchants, citing heavy costs, are keen to sell, so market prices are inevitably grading lower quality rice as medium and medium as high, resulting in an invisible rise in market prices. Genuine high-quality rice is met with mutual observation due to price limits. Early rice stocks are running low, and sales are brisk, with prices rising by a fraction of a cent. Top grade is opening at 19 taels. Sales of Yang Xian [Indica rice] are slightly slower, but prices remain firm. Du Xian [another type of Indica rice] is arriving and being sold immediately. The general market remained stable in the afternoon after news of a weakening foreign rice market. Bai Yuan [White Round-Grain rice] is gradually improving, with slight movement in customer sales and a slightly better price, up almost a cent.

▲ South Shanghai: Not much coming from the river area, and the market remains active. Sales of machine-milled white Japonica rice from Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Tongzhou vary slightly. However, a significant amount of rice is being shipped out of the interior of Pudong. Local merchants and customers are carefully buying up the rice. Merchants from Chongming, Qidong, and Tongzhou are also keen to buy, because after the sharp rise in foreign rice prices, they have mostly switched to buying rice from Tongli and other areas. As a result, Japonica rice prices here have risen by a fraction of a cent. Sales of Changzhou rice are normal. It has been determined that after the authorities established the Rice Price Stabilization Committee, it has now begun operations. It is unknown whether the grain market will shrink in the future. The prices of Southern early rice are all rising accordingly. Indica rice remains tight, and stores are eager to stock it. The market continues to be firm. Buying interest in Tongbian Yin Hua [a type of rice] is also improving. The situation is initially stable and then strengthens. Top grade rice is opening at 17 yuan and 8 jiao [角, 1/10 of a yuan].

Foreign Rice Futures and Spot Prices Both Fall 196

Yesterday, foreign rice suddenly turned weak. Because of the upcoming customs closure today and the holiday the day after tomorrow [Sunday], customers are temporarily suspending business for customs clearance. The total market only opened with over 2,000 bags of spot goods. With few transactions, people's hearts were soft, and many were eager to dispose of their positions. Prices of various rice fell by a small amount, from 1 jiao to 1 jiao and a half. Number One Saigon was 15 yuan and 6 jiao, small size 15 yuan, large size 14 yuan and 8 jiao. Futures followed spot prices in the same downward trend, falling by 4-5 fen [分, 1/100 of a yuan] to 7-8 fen. However, transactions were still good, with a total of over 2,000 tons opened in the market, of which small-size rice accounted for more than half, it is said.

Clear Weather Causes New Vermicelli to Fall Slightly 197

Yesterday, the vermicelli market showed a trend of near-term strength and long-term weakness. For the current month, because the delivery date is approaching, the largest manufacturers have consistently maintained a "no-selling" policy. It is said that the major manufacturers have fully repurchased their contracts on the exchange side for this month. Although the smaller manufacturers have not repurchased their positions, the bulls have the major manufacturers as their backing and are not loosening their grip. Therefore, the current month is showing a small profit. As for long-term new vermicelli, due to the favorable weather, it is naturally softening in this sunny weather. Customers in Suzhou, Changzhou, and Jiangbei are selling actively, taking advantage of the good weather. It is said that only the Wuxi gang is stubbornly holding on. The shift in the future trend still depends on the weather as the key, because this kind of situation is almost entirely due to the psychological effect. As a result, the current month rose by 1 fen compared to the previous day, May rose by 2.5 li [厘, 1/1000 of a tael], June rose by 5 li, and July to September each fell by 7.5 li, it is said.

Main Reasons for the Recovery of the Wheat Market 198

▲ Foreign Wheat Prices Rise ··· Wuxi Gang Absorbs ··· Factory Purchases Also Eager

Yesterday, the wheat market improved because foreign wheat prices had slightly recovered. In addition, the Wuxi gang ultimately felt that rice prices were becoming increasingly expensive. Considering the price ratio, the demand for new wheat remained very strong. According to industry insiders, the Wuxi gang had made huge profits on foreign rice this year, both in futures and spot, so their absorption of wheat was also smooth. They were not initially concerned about whether they would lose money. According to this situation, it is said that the inland gangs will not let go until June reaches 4 taels and 6 qian [錢, 1/10 of a tael]. As a result, the current month rose by 3 fen compared to the previous day, June rose by 1 fen, July remained unchanged, and August and September each rose by 2 fen. Spot wheat remained in demand from factories, and regardless of high or low quality, they were quite eager to buy. Therefore, asking prices were about 2-3 fen better than the previous day. Kainam, Suzhou, and Bengbu wheat were offered at 5 taels and 1 qian, 5 taels, 6-7 fen. Jiangxi and Hankou wheat were offered at 5 taels, 4 taels and 8 qian, 8 fen, 4 taels and 8 qian, and 4 taels and 7 qian and 5 fen, for a total of over 8,600 bags, which were purchased by Fuxin and Fufeng factories, it is said.

Silk and Tea: Low Opening Price for Mulberry Leaves in Wuxi 199

▲ Mulberry Trees Damaged by Weather ··· Price Only 2 Yuan, Few Transactions

Wuxi is a famous sericulture area in China. Raising silkworms and planting mulberry trees is a sideline for farmers. There are many mulberry fields in the surrounding villages. Last winter, due to the severe cold weather and heavy frost, the mulberry trees were damaged. During the Qingming Festival, the mulberry trees were budding, and the mulberry buds were beaten off by thunder and hail, and the leaf production will inevitably be greatly affected. Farmers in various cities and towns are in the process of hatching silkworm eggs. In view of this situation, they are rushing to buy silkworm ant feed. The mulberry leaf market opened at only 2 yuan per dan [担, a unit of weight], and few transactions were made. The leaf households are all waiting for a good price to sell. Due to the high prices demanded by Chinese merchants in the Shanghai silk market, transactions continued to be slow. Only Dachang and others brought in 30 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, and Xinfu and others brought in 30 packages of Baigan silk. Prices are all firm.

Preventing Meningitis by Zhu Yang-gao 202

Meningitis is now even more rampant, endangering countless lives. The reason for this is the underdevelopment of our country's sanitation facilities. Meningitis is caused by the invasion of the body by the Meningitis bacteria. Patients become a colony for the bacteria, where it develops and reproduces. Although the body's resistance fights against it, it is often unable to win. Patients are full of germs, and all bodily excrement contains them. The most dangerous are saliva and nasal mucus. When speaking or coughing, liquid droplets containing germs are often sprayed on others. Therefore, about 30% of the people around the patient contain these germs. These germ carriers (medically called post-germ carriers) may or may not get sick, depending on the thickness of their resistance. If they are lucky enough not to get sick, and still work in society and come into contact with others, they can transmit the germs in their mouths to others. This third person who gets the germs often gets sick, and the rate of illness is higher than that of the second person who directly receives the germs from the patient, because the germs can always increase their toxicity in the body of the second person. In summary, these germ-carrying people who are not sick are the most important spreaders of Meningitis, and are also the most dangerous to society, because one person can cause thousands of people to get the germs and get sick. Therefore, if we want to eradicate Meningitis, we must first teach these people not to allow others to come into contact with them, and to suspend their duties until the germs are checked twice and not found, and then they can resume their duties as usual. The person himself should be disinfected under the guidance of a doctor. After about three weeks, all the germs can be eliminated. Although there may be some losses in business, the benefits to society are not small. The second most important thing to prevent this disease is to isolate the sick in one place, or in a hospital, so that they cannot create germ carriers. Also, the patient's belongings, clothing, etc., must be disinfected at any time. After recovery (or death), the ward must also be completely disinfected to prevent endangering society. For example, when doing laundry, do not directly hand the patient's clothes to the laundry worker. It must first be soaked in a stinky water solution for about 2 hours before handing it over.

Attached Disinfection Method

Disinfection of mouth, nose, and hands: Wash with one tablespoon of hydrogen peroxide added to one cup of warm water. Wash hands with 3% Lysol soap and water.

Disinfection of clothing, etc.: Immerse in 5% carbolic acid solution for at least 2 hours.

Disinfection of woolen clothing: Because it cannot be immersed in water, spray it with 3% Lysol solution and sprinkle it in the sunlight.

Disinfection of cheap toys, paper goods, etc.: Burn them.

Disinfection of wards: Repaint the walls with lime water. Wash floors and wooden objects with hot lye water and soap, or wash with 5% carbolic acid solution.

▲ Dr. Feng Baiyuan is a member of the China Medical Association and has passed the Health Bureau examination and is authorized to register. He is uniquely skilled in medicine and has superb medical skills. All difficult and complicated diseases treated by him are effectively cured. He is especially knowledgeable in gynecology, pediatrics, and venereal diseases. At the request of his relatives and friends, he will share his more than 30 years of experience and start seeing patients at Huxie, Sanduo Lane, North Sichuan Road, on the 14th of this month.

Theater News 204

▲ Central Grand Theater announces: Starting today, our theater will screen the famous European epic film "Robin Hood Lissen". This film is based on the famous Russian poem, telling the story of Lissen, a 17th-century Russian Volga River pirate. It is generous, passionate, and moving. It depicts a hero who is not burdened by lust but ultimately harmed by it, truly moving heroes around the world to tears. The entire film took more than two years to produce, with thousands of actors. The temporary filming location was the German Zeppelin airfield, where a river channel more than 2,000 feet wide was excavated. Movie stars from Germany, Russia, England, and France were carefully selected to play the leading and supporting roles in the film. It is a masterpiece of the great Russian director Toronski.

▲ Xinxin Garden, Nanjing Road announces: Our Qiankun Living Drama Troupe previously performed the Qing palace secret history "Empress Dowager Cixi," which caused a sensation in Shanghai. Now, we are restaging the complete social drama "Living Buddha Jigong," which is currently being performed continuously. The plot is exquisite, the performances are realistic, and the mechanical sets are mysterious and ingenious. As a result, the theater is always full. The troupe is preparing five or six more episodes, which have been rehearsed thoroughly. Many strange mechanical sets have been added and are scheduled to be performed starting this Saturday.

▲ Paris Grand Theater announces: Starting today, we will screen the war epic "The Soul of France." This film depicts the bravery and endurance of French soldiers during the European War, with the Great War as the background. The entire film is based on patriotism and woven with compassion, which is deeply moving and even more spectacular than "Four Sons Join the Army."

▲ Xifan Film Company announces: Our company's martial arts productions have always been famous in various ports at home and abroad. Recently, following the "Three Great Knights," our company has produced the martial arts romance "Wandering Swordsman." The plot is tortuous and interesting, the performances of the male and female actors are delicate and realistic, the cinematography is novel and varied, and the sets are magnificent. It is definitely the first choice. This film stars actresses Wang Feijuan, Tang Xueqian, and Ai Yajuan. The three ladies are all skilled in martial arts, and each has her own strengths in the play, all with amazing skills.

▲ Golden Grand Theater announces: The American film industry has produced many comedians, especially the up-and-coming Sammy Cohen, who specializes in facial expressions of foolishness, is the most popular. His big nose and facial features are unique, making people laugh at first sight. His adventurous and ingenious performances are unmatched by other comedians. You can see everything in the film "Trouble in the Palace," which will be shown at the Golden Grand Theater today.

▲ Star Film Company announces: The Hangzhou National Games has commissioned our film company to exclusively produce the sports film of the event. Our company has dispatched several photographers with multiple cameras to the venue to film. From the opening to the closing ceremony, we have filmed more than 12,000 feet of film. All the opening ceremony, men's and women's track and field events, various rescue events, and various sports have been filmed completely and meticulously. Now, our company is editing the film and adding appropriate and moving subtitles. It will be completed soon and is scheduled to be premiered at the Central Grand Theater on the 27th of this month for sports enthusiasts.

▲ Feifei Girls' Dance Troupe announces: Our troupe is scheduled to hold its inaugural meeting at the Penglai Grand Theater, Xiaoximen, on April 22. Tickets are priced at 40 cents and 60 cents. There is also a special ticket, priced at two yuan for a book of nine. Major bookstores in this city are selling them.

▲ Zhang Lancun, a lay Buddhist from Hexian, Anhui, is skilled in calligraphy and proficient in poetry. He has moved to the opposite side of the Xinwen Daily office on Sanma Road and re-established his fee schedule. Those who admire the lay Buddhist's calligraphy should not miss the opportunity.

Expansion of Shanghai Art College 207

The Shanghai Art College on Jiangwan Road (formerly the China Art Academy) is a newly established art institution. Recently, in order to change students' artistic interests, a spring study tour was held. One group went to West Lake in Hangzhou, and the other group stayed in Suzhou. They departed on the 14th of this month. Mr. Wang Daoyuan, the organizer of the school, in order to establish the foundation of the school, has purchased several acres of land and several large buildings near Tiantong'an in this city (which were repurchased from the Japanese). With the assistance of enthusiastic educators, the new school building can probably be completed before the next semester begins. In order to supplement the talents for social construction in our country, the school has decided to add design and architecture departments next semester. From the establishment of the school to the present, only a few months have passed, and all plans have been so rapidly fulfilled. It is truly a dawn for the art world in our country.

Highest Radio Station in American Architecture 208

The Radio Corporation of America is building a new building, 50 stories high, located at the intersection of Lexington Avenue and East 21st Street. It will be completed in mid-May next year. The building is in the style of an ancient church, with a spire towering into the clouds. The top of the tower is equipped with a radio station, which is the tallest in the world. At night, the top of the spire is illuminated with colorful lights, which is extremely brilliant and represents the spirit of radio. It is also a scenic spot in the whole city. After the new building is built, most of it will be the office of the Radio Corporation of America. The scale is grand, and it is said that the construction cost is more than 7.5 million yuan.

German Government Commemorates Dr. Stresemann 209

▲ Renaming a Major Street in Berlin

Berlin News: Berlin has a major street called Koniggratz Street, which was named 50 years ago to commemorate Germany's victory over the Austrian army in the Battle of Koniggratz. Recently, it has been renamed Stresemann Street by government order to commemorate the late Foreign Minister Dr. Stresemann, while simultaneously eliminating a negative old impression between Germany and Austria. It's a win-win situation.

Grand Plan for Direct Canal between Central Europe 210

▲ From the North Sea to the Black Sea

▲ Construction is Progressing Rapidly

Vienna News: A very large excavation project is currently underway here. The content of this project is to open a waterway across Europe, from the North Sea to the Black Sea, passing through the Rhine, Main, and Danube rivers. The direct shipping route from the Rhine to the Danube was opened in 1864, but because the riverbed is not deep, only ships of 120 tons can travel. In 1901, the Rhine-Main-Danube Joint Company was organized to plan a canal between the North Sea and the Black Sea, so that large ships could travel. The company first opened a 70-mile-long river channel on the upper reaches of the Danube River from Passau. In 1926, the dredging work of the Main River began in Aschaffenburg, Bavaria, Germany. It has now been opened to Miltenberg and is expected to be opened to Wurzburg by 1937. On the other hand, the Danube River work from Passau to the Black Sea is also progressing slowly. In the future, after the completion of this grand canal, transportation in Central Europe will be greatly facilitated. Hungary, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Bulgaria all hope to use this waterway to transport agricultural products at low cost and import industrial products. After the completion of the canal, it is estimated that it can generate 168,202 kilowatts of hydroelectric power per year, as a by-product, for industrial use. After the opening of the Elbe-Oder-Danube canal, which is under discussion, Czechoslovakia and Poland can be connected with the Balkan Peninsula and Southern Russia. The Danube River will occupy an increasingly important position.

Newspapers around the World Published Simultaneously at the Same Time 211

▲ Possible in the Future

Schenectady News: Charles Young, son of Owen Young, who is famous for the Young Plan, invented a wireless telegraphy machine. Recently, he used this machine to record the records of the San Francisco Call-Bulletin published in San Francisco. Within three hours of the newspaper's publication, the electric transmission crossed the continent, and its front page was completely received. Charles Young stated in a speech that he hopes that in the future, a page of the London Times can be transmitted to New York in a "flash." Therefore, some people predict that in the future, newspapers around the world can be published simultaneously at the same time.

US National Census Begins 212

▲ Budget is about 12,200,000

Washington News: The US National Census began on the 2nd of this month. There are a total of 100,000 surveyors dispatched from various states. The estimated total population of the United States is 12.2 million.

Social News Submission Guidelines 213

(1) Articles are limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural areas, health, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life.

(2) Pictures are limited to various lyrical paintings about social life.

(3) Photographs are qualified if they are of seasons, scenery, flora and fauna, people, and news-related photography. Seasonal landscape photography, especially of ladies, is especially welcome.

(4) Each article should not exceed 2,000 words.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally. Write neatly. Western text should be omitted where possible. If the original text must be quoted, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for drawings, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate "Social News Department" when submitting manuscripts.

(9) All manuscripts will not be returned, whether published or not. If you need them to be returned, please state this in advance and attach sufficient postage.
